Current Commentary

Twists and Turns in the Shaanxi Situation and Mediation

— Du

The Shaanxi-Gansu problem, which once caused great concern, has recently taken a sharp turn for the better. The central government has repeatedly declared its intention to be lenient, and Zhang and Yang's troops have also been withdrawing in succession in compliance with orders. The gloom of the situation is gradually dissipating, and the people are finally catching their breath. Just when there were expectations of a smooth and orderly progression without any obstacles, unexpectedly, unpredictable changes emerged again. The city gates of Xi'an were closed, and the sound of gunfire suddenly arose from within, causing the remaining people to suffer another round of panic. The nearly completed agreement suffered an unexpected setback. This was something that ordinary people could never have foreseen. Although this incident was quickly suppressed, and order in Xi'an has been restored, the underlying anxiety in people's hearts has not been eliminated, and the potential for further unrest remains. Since the Shaanxi Incident occurred, there have been so many twists and turns that it has been difficult to resolve, demonstrating the difficulty of dealing with the aftermath.

The truth of this internal strife in Xi'an is still unclear. It is said that it was due to radical elements among the officers of Zhang's troops, who were dissatisfied with the terms of the peaceful resolution and wanted to use coercion to obtain commitments from senior generals to continue their attitude of opposition to the central government. After the senior generals sternly refused, the uprising broke out. Wang Yizhe, the commander of the 67th Army of the Northeast Army, was killed, and the chief of the adjutant's office, Song Xueli, and two others died along with him. After Yang Hucheng, Yu Xuezhong, and others tried their best to suppress and persuade them, the other troops, angered by Wang's murder, also rose up in opposition. The rioting elements began to retreat outside the city, and the turmoil gradually subsided. Although this matter is not directly related to the central government's handling of the aftermath, at a time when the national crisis is urgent, and we are relying on concentrating all our efforts to serve the country, this unfortunate incident has occurred, foreshadowing a division and weakening of our strength, causing a blow to our morale. And a valiant and skilled general like Wang Yizhe died not on the battlefield, but as a victim of assassination, which is a major loss for the country. Who would not feel distressed and uneasy about this?

The incident arose suddenly and was quelled just as suddenly. On the one hand, this shows the extreme actions of the radical elements, and on the other hand, it shows that there are still many people who understand the situation. However, the greatest driving force, the weight of the invisible mediation, should still be attributed to the collective will of the entire country. The collective will demands unity and peace, and no matter what kind of force rises, it cannot be allowed to repeat the destruction of peace before the external goal has been abandoned. Any action that divides unity will ultimately yield to this collective will. Otherwise, with the lax discipline and chaotic situation of Zhang and Yang's troops, which had already caused a deteriorating situation, how could it have been quelled in such a short period of time? Is it not the collective will for peace and unity that has influenced this? This is true of this incident, and it has been true of past events as well. If the strength of the collective will is not destroyed, there is hope for the restoration of the country's fortunes.

Eden Goes to Southern France for Two Weeks of Rest

His duties are delegated to the Prime Minister.

[London] British Foreign Secretary Eden is scheduled to depart for southern France on Saturday for a two-week vacation. During his absence, the position of Foreign Secretary will be temporarily assumed by Lord Privy Seal Viscount Halifax. (Central News Agency, Reuters dispatch, 4th)

[London] Regarding Foreign Secretary Eden's departure to southern France for a two-week rest, the Morning Post recently commented that, "Since German leader Hitler delivered his speech on the 30th of last month, there have been many important unresolved issues, such as Germany's demand for the restoration of its former colonies, which are urgent matters to be dealt with. It is rather strange for the Foreign Secretary to take a vacation at this time. As for his deputy, 'Lord Privy Seal Viscount Halifax, although he has repeatedly served as Acting Foreign Secretary, he is known to have more sympathy for Germany than Foreign Secretary Eden.'" (Havas dispatch, 5th)

Japanese Army Authorities Eager to Implement New National Defense Plan

Recognize the Urgent Need to Develop Industry; China and Japan Seek to Implement Economic Cooperation

[Nanjing] Based on the new national defense preparation plan, the Japanese army authorities are attempting to achieve a substantial enhancement of military strength. In order to implement this plan, a strong government is of course necessary, but the army hopes that the Hayashi Cabinet will first decide on its fundamental policy. According to the army's opinion, domestic industry is the foundation of the new national defense enhancement plan, so it places emphasis on its development, and links the development of "Manchukuo" industry with the new national defense enhancement plan as inseparable. It will strive to solve problems closely related to national defense, such as aviation, electricity, fuel, and steelmaking. For this purpose, it will create state organs such as the Ministry of Trade, or establish large semi-official and semi-private trading companies to promote the overseas development of Japanese goods. Therefore, the trend of Japanese politics and economy should also implement major transformations according to this policy. The diplomatic policy towards China should also be based on the harmony of Eastern nations, strengthen Sino-Japanese economic cooperation, and when the new national defense enhancement plan is completed, it will ease the previous exclusive policy towards the North, and focus on the Southern policy. (Allied Press dispatch, 5th)

Japanese Parliament Expected Not to Dissolve; New Cabinet Quickly Establishes Concrete Plans

[Tokyo] The Hayashi Senjuro Cabinet is currently undertaking to establish concrete policies with the greatest speed. It is heard that there is a greater possibility that the parliament will not be dissolved. The Ministry of the Army seems to no longer insist on its original position of dissolving the parliament, hoping to restore normalcy as soon as possible. Fearing widespread rumors that some within the government still advocate dissolving the parliament, more than forty members of the House of Representatives, led by veteran politician Yukio Ozaki (all of whom are not members of the Seiyukai and Minseito parties), submitted a memorandum to the parliament regarding the dissolution of the parliament, rejecting the concept of dissolving the parliament in a way that is unconstitutional, but it is generally believed that this move is only a demonstration. Most of the Seiyukai and Minseito parties do not want to make the situation more complicated, so it is generally believed that after the parliament reopens, if no unexpected events suddenly occur, the situation can be safely passed, and this belief is growing. The candidate for Foreign Minister does not want to be selected before the parliament reopens. The leaders of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs recently submitted a program for reforming Japan's foreign policy to Prime Minister Hayashi for his reference. (Central News Agency dispatch, 5th)

Saito Hiroshi Indicates He Will Not Accept Foreign Minister Post

[Washington] Japanese Ambassador to the United States Hiroshi Saito announced today that he has decided not to accept the post of Foreign Minister in the Hayashi Cabinet and will remain in his current position as ambassador. (National News dispatch, 4th)

Ministry of Finance Tentatively Abandons Baba Tax Plan

To be revised and resubmitted to Parliament

[Nanjing] The Ministry of Finance held a meeting of the Tax Bureau at the Minister's official residence on the afternoon of the 4th. After discussing the previous cabinet's tax reform plan, in view of the actual situation of the financial world and the opinions of various parties, it was recognized that the original plan was not suitable for implementation. Therefore, it was decided to revise it during the parliamentary recess and submit it to the parliament. The fundamental direction of the revision is to alleviate the excessive burden on the people, while at the same time trying not to reduce tax revenue. Two concrete methods are proposed: ㊀ completely abolish Minister Baba's original reform plan and implement a simple increase in tax rates based on the current tax law, while adding some new taxes; ㊁ base on Minister Baba's original plan, modify the inappropriate parts and new taxes, or eliminate useless parts. After discussion, it seems that it was decided to abandon the Baba original plan, base on the current tax law, and adopt the method of increasing taxes and setting up new taxes. In that case, the first type of the second kind of income tax and its combined taxation on the third kind will of course be implemented moderately. Regarding the new tax issue, in Minister Baba's original plan, the transaction tax should be abolished, the property tax should also be completely abolished, or only the part of increasing taxes for corporations should be retained. As for the foreign currency debt, special debt, and securities transfer tax, all will be subject to considerable revisions. Regarding the trade control tax and export control tax, there is still a strong opinion on setting it up. The Ministry of Finance intends to re-examine the national tax and local tax revisions because they are related to the local financial adjustment allocation. (Allied Press dispatch, 5th)

Prime Minister Hayashi Selects Full-Time Cabinet Members

[Tokyo] The current Cabinet members of the Hayashi Cabinet, such as Yuki, Yamazaki, and Godo, are mostly concurrent cabinet members. However, in preparation for the reopening of parliament, the Hayashi Cabinet plans to quickly find suitable talents and set up full-time cabinet members in the ministries that are currently held concurrently. It is in the process of searching for candidates, and it has been internally decided to set up a full-time Minister of Communications before the parliament reopens. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the Ministry of Education are also scheduled to set up full-time ministers at appropriate times, but the Minister of Railways and the Minister of Colonial Affairs will be temporarily held concurrently by cabinet members. (Allied Press dispatch, 5th)

Japanese Shipbuilding Industry Booming

Steel Mills Plan to Increase Production

[Tokyo] Last year, Japanese shipyards received orders for a total of 116 new ships, with a gross weight of 736,250 tons. Ships under 1,000 tons have not been included. At the end of last year, there were a total of 142 ships, totaling 836,950 tons, either under construction or scheduled to begin construction this year. However, due to the shortage of steel, many orders cannot be fulfilled as scheduled. The Ministry of Commerce and Industry currently estimates that the total amount of steel needed in Japan from April this year to the end of March next year is approximately 500,000 tons. Nippon Steel Corporation and several other steel companies have expanded their factory facilities, so it is expected that production can be increased soon to meet the needs of the country. The Ministry of Commerce and Industry currently believes that the recent rise in steel prices is due to manipulation by speculators. (Central News Agency, Reuters dispatch, 5th)

US Naval Construction Plan

Faces Stagnation Due to Dispute Between Government and Business

[Washington] The US naval construction plan is on the verge of stagnation due to a dispute between the government and the business community. It is said that steel mills and steel manufacturers are not supplying the necessary materials to the naval authorities as a form of protest against the Walsh-Healey Act. The Act stipulates a 40-hour work week, and this provision and other measures must be observed by manufacturers who want to undertake government projects. However, the steel mills are currently operating at full capacity, and even with a 48-hour work week, they are unable to meet the demand, and are reluctant to reduce working hours by accepting government projects. Government projects are smaller than private orders, and the manufacturers feel that it is not worth it to reduce working hours by accepting government projects. Furthermore, the Navy Department recently announced a tender to purchase 2,735,000 pounds of copper. The authorities received bids for 1,035,000 pounds, but the government could only purchase 885,000 pounds, the rest of which did not comply with the provisions of the Walsh-Healey Act. On December 4th of last year, the naval authorities again wanted to purchase 25 million pounds of steel, but the manufacturers only submitted bids for 7 million pounds, and all had to be rejected because they violated the Walsh-Healey Act. In this situation, if there are no other developments recently, the planned construction of two battleships, each with 35,000 tons, will be impossible to start. The Portsmouth Naval Shipyard, which is currently building several submarines, is likely to shut down, and the materials stored at the Washington Navy Yard are also gradually becoming scarce. It is reported that the naval authorities consulted with Labor Secretary Perkins, that the manufacturers' bids for steel could be temporarily exempted from complying with the Walsh-Healey Act, but Perkins refused to accept this method, and labor leader Lewis fundamentally opposed this method. (Central News Agency, Reuters dispatch, 4th)

French Three-Year Naval Construction Program

Under Consideration by Authorities

[Paris] Naval correspondent Laborie of the "Petit Parisien" newspaper recently published an article on the French Navy, stating that the total tonnage of the national navy is currently 630,000 tons, and is expected to increase to 850,000 tons within a few years, including many of the latest warships. To prevent delays in naval construction, the government intends to request that the parliament pass the naval construction program for the next three years at the same time. Because parliamentary debates on naval construction programs often take a long time, this is the main reason for past delays in naval construction. For example, although the battleship "Dunkerque" is the most superior warship in the world, construction only began after eighteen months of parliamentary debate, due to the opposition of the majority party members to the construction of battleships several years ago. The delay is evident. Furthermore, since the parliament passed a law stipulating that workers should work 40 hours per week, although the number of workers in shipyards has increased by 11%, they still need to work overtime to make up for the shortfall. The government should also train skilled workers to meet urgent needs. As for the government's three-year naval construction program, it is currently under study. The content will roughly include the following types of warships: ⑴ One or two 15,000-ton aircraft carriers, capable of carrying 40 aircraft, with a speed of 30 knots per hour; ⑵ Several 8,000-ton cruisers; ⑶ A squadron of torpedo boats; ⑷ Ten or so first-class and second-class submarines. (Havas dispatch from the 5th)

Asian Labor Conference to be Convened

Council of State Drafts Report Recommending Three Items for Agenda

[Geneva] At the International Labor Conference held in June of last year, a proposal put forward by labor representatives from India and Japan was passed, advocating the convening of an Asian Labor Conference in Asia to seek to develop cooperation between Asian countries and the International Labor Office. It was decided that the Council of the International Labor Office should draft a report. The report has now been drafted and will be jointly reviewed tomorrow by the Asian members of the Council of the International Labor Office. It is reported that the report suggests including the following three issues on the agenda of the Asian Labor Conference: ⑴ The issue of Asian countries participating in the International Labor Organization; ⑵ The impact of industrial development and population conditions in Asian countries on immigration issues; ⑶ The issue of establishing a permanent labor committee for Asian countries. The report also argues that in addition to the participation of countries such as Afghanistan, China, India, Iran, Iraq, Japan, and Siam, the Asian Labor Conference should also include colonial powers from Europe and the Americas, such as the United States, Britain, France, the Netherlands, and Portugal. As for the expenses of the Asian Labor Conference, if held in Tokyo, Japan, it would cost approximately 275,000 Swiss francs; if held in Mumbai, India, it would cost approximately 200,000 Swiss francs. (Havas dispatch from the 3rd)

British Regency Bill

Passed Third Reading in Lower House

[London] The Regency Bill was unanimously passed for the third reading in the Lower House tonight. When the bill was under consideration by the review committee in the Lower House, it agreed to the amendment proposed by Home Secretary Simon, that is, increasing the necessary number of people required to declare that the monarch is unable to perform his duties and needs to appoint a regent from three to four. However, it was later fixed at three, and the number of people with the power to declare was reduced to five, in order to remove one person who could be a regent. Simon also proposed an amendment, deleting the phrase "the regent should reside in Britain" and replacing it with "should be residing in any part of Britain," in case the appointed regent happens to be serving as the Governor-General of a dominion or temporarily residing in a dominion. This section was also approved by the committee. Simon also stated that in the event that the Emperor travels abroad or is temporarily unable to govern, the State Council should be composed of the Queen, the Duke of Gloucester, the Duke of Kent, the Princess Royal, and Prince Connaught. (Reuters dispatch from Central News Agency, the 4th)

U.S. Pacific Coast Sailors Return to Work

Strike Lasts 98 Days with Significant Losses; Workers Vote to Approve Interim Measures

[San Francisco] The Sailors' Strike Committee today notified shipping companies on the Pacific Coast that the sailors' strike, which has lasted three months and caused the stagnation of shipping in various ports on the West Coast and Honolulu, has been completely resolved, and the striking sailors will return to work in full force at 8:00 a.m. tomorrow. The Joint Committee of the Union also confirmed this news, stating that union workers have completed voting and the majority have approved of ending the strike, so the labor unrest has indeed ended. However, this worker vote did not include firemen, oilers, and cleaners, but the departure of ships will not be delayed as a result. It is reported that the Pacific Coast maritime strike has lasted for 98 days, with losses estimated at around 100 million yuan. The general public is very happy about the end of the strike, but this resumption of work is in fact only a truce, not permanent peace. Several issues remain unresolved, including: ⑴ Firemen's union workers are still dissatisfied with the terms negotiated by the union representatives and the shipping association; ⑵ The strike by barge workers in Los Angeles and San Francisco has not yet been resolved; ⑶ Shipyard workers in San Francisco and Seattle are still on strike; ⑷ Dockworkers in Honolulu are difficult to deal with; ⑸ Weighers, clerks, and inspectors on the West Coast have unanimously expressed dissatisfaction with the previously established agreement. Among them, the firemen's strike is more serious, with 1,234 firemen opposing the return to work terms and only 857 in favor, but all agree to temporarily resume work and then resolve the issues of wages and working conditions. Shipping companies and firemen have both informally expressed hope for a satisfactory resolution. (Dispatch from the 4th, National News)

[San Francisco] The maritime unions of various U.S. Pacific ports, which went on strike on October 30th of last year due to disputes with employers over wages and employment methods, declared a resolution today after 98 days. The sailors have agreed to return to work immediately. It is reported that this labor unrest spread widely, and maritime unions in various ports along the Atlantic coast also implemented slowdowns in support. During the Pacific ports sailors' strike, commerce stagnated, and even Hawaii and Alaska were affected, with travelers stranded and food supplies running out. The losses suffered by the shipping companies were naturally considerable. Subsequently, the Shipping Commission, the Shipping Association, and the maritime unions conducted negotiations, and it was decided on the 31st of last month that the sailors would hold a vote to resolve the issue. By the time the voting results came out, the sailors had unanimously accepted the interim measures, and the labor unrest that had been delayed for more than three months came to an end. (Havas dispatch from the 4th)

Italy Prepares to Sign Non-Aggression Pact with Balkan Countries

Southern Army of 1.5 Million Ready for Anything; Italy and Yugoslavia Repair Old Ties, a Factor for Peace in Central Europe

Turkish Capital: Official sources have revealed that after Foreign Minister Rushdi, in his capacity as Turkish Foreign Minister and Chairman of the Standing Political Council of the Balkan Entente, held talks with Italian Foreign Minister Ciano, Italy, Turkey, Yugoslavia, and Greece are likely to sign an Eastern Mediterranean Mutual Assistance and Non-Aggression Pact in the near future. German Ambassador Performs Nazi Salute to British King

Violates Diplomatic Conventions

[London] When King George VI received ambassadors and ministers from various countries at Buckingham Palace yesterday, the German Ambassador to Britain, Ribbentrop, performed a Nazi salute to him. All the newspapers have commented on this. The Daily Herald reported, "When the palace staff announced the name of the German Ambassador Ribbentrop, the ambassador immediately stepped forward several paces, stood at attention, and extended his right hand, performing a Nazi salute to the King. Then he advanced three steps, stood at attention, and extended his right hand again. Finally, he advanced one step, stood at attention, and saluted as before. The King responded with a bow." The News Chronicle reported, "This incident has caused unease in diplomatic circles. Ribbentrop may resign and return home. Although there are many powerful figures in the British Conservative Party who are friendly with him, most cabinet members said that the ambassador's actions were propaganda for National Socialism and had violated diplomatic conventions. In addition, the ambassador has been traveling between London and Berlin since taking office, failing to reside in his post for a long time, which is also inappropriate. Moreover, the ambassador even participated in drafting the speech given by his head of state Hitler in the House of Commons on the 30th of last month, which is well known to people in Downing Street and therefore makes them dissatisfied." (Havas dispatch from the 5th)

In other words, regarding the neutral status of Belgium and the Netherlands, Germany only made empty and general declarations, without providing any concrete suggestions. Disputes over Hunan's Construction of Tianhu Polder and Manganese Mines Near Xiamen Encroaching on Dongting Lake

People in Hunan and Hubei Provinces Voice Opposition; Yangtze River Water Conservancy Commission Sends Personnel for Thorough Investigation

Hankou Correspondence – Dongting Lake is a natural reservoir of the Yangtze River. Recently, Hunan Province constructed Tianhu Polder, encroaching on 13% of the existing lake area. This water conservancy issue has caused significant political waves in Hunan Province. The resignation of Finance Director He Hao, and the proposed partial reorganization of the Hunan Provincial Government, are due to this reason. As for Hubei Province, there is even more public outcry because it is "making a drain for itself at the expense of its neighbor." The Yangtze River Water Conservancy Commission also attaches great importance to this matter and has specially dispatched the Director of the Engineering Department, Sun Liangshi, to Hankou yesterday to go to Hunan for a thorough investigation. It is expected that there will be an appropriate solution in the shortest period. Previously, Ye Kaixin, a senator of the Military Council, returned to Hunan at the end of last year and, together with the old Tianhu Polder directors, borrowed 500,000 yuan from the Hunan Provincial Bank to build Tianhu Polder. The polder covers an area of over 400,000 mu, approximately 13% of the existing Dongting Lake area. The first to oppose it was the Hunan Flood Relief Committee, whose rationale was that they have been planning Dongting Lake water conservancy for years. Although they have not been able to carry out large-scale dredging due to funding issues, local projects such as the Zhucikou diversion canal, widening of the Hao River and the Linzi and Liangko openings, and the establishment of hydrological stations have been carried out successively and have been somewhat effective. Now, suddenly, while talking about water conservancy, they are building Tianhu Polder, reclaiming Datu Lake, and blocking part of the existing entire lake area. How is this different from building a lake on one side and blocking a lake on the other, preventing disasters on one side and creating disasters on the other? Therefore, a meeting of the entire committee was convened, and it was decided to send a letter to the Hunan Provincial Government to request relief, so as to preserve the lake area and reduce disasters. The Hunan Provincial Government then invited Hunan University professor and Flood Relief Committee engineer Xiao Guangjiong, together with committee member Zhou Fengjiu, to conduct a survey. According to the report, it was also believed that the polder should not be built. Other oppositions followed, like clouds rising. The people of the counties along the river in Hubei Province believe that if the polder is built, the water storage capacity of Dongting Lake will naturally decrease. If the Yangtze River rises and Dongting cannot accommodate it, it will drive eastward, and Hubei Province will bear the brunt. The massive disaster that will be caused in the future will not be comparable to that of the 20th year of the Republic. This policy of benefiting oneself at the expense of one's neighbor is absolutely unacceptable, and a telegram has been sent to all parties resolutely opposing it. Recently, the Hubei Provincial Water Conservancy Authority expressed its opinion on the matter, stating, "Dongting Lake is the original natural reservoir in the Hunan and Hubei regions, relying on Songzi, Taiping, Ouchi, Tiaoxian, and Chenglingji and Hukou, to regulate the flow of the river. The original water storage area of the lake was 6,780 square kilometers, of which 2,340 square kilometers were occupied by polders, accounting for more than one-third of the total area. Moreover, the lake fields in Yiyang, Xiangyin, Yuanjiang, Hanshou, Nanxian, Changde, Huarong, Anxiang, Lixian, Yueyang, and Linxiang, which border the lake, account for more than 50% of the cultivated land in these counties. Every time a silt island appears, the gentry and wealthy people individually or jointly obtain licenses from the Lake Field Bureau, paying only a few jiao per mu, and then they can reclaim it. According to the Anxiang County Chronicle, during the Daoguang and Tongzhi years, Anxiang had only 14 lake polders. Fifty years ago, there were only over one hundred polders. Now, Anxiang has reached more than six hundred and thirty lake polders, with a total cultivated area of over 600,000 mu. The establishment of Nanxian County is only forty years in history. Initially, it should be in the ninth capital of Huarong, called Nanzhou Hall. Later, siltation increased daily, cultivated land gradually increased, and the population became more numerous, so the county seat was changed. The speed of new polders can be seen from this. The unplanned construction of Tianhu Polder this time is actually competing with water for land, making the reservoir smaller and smaller, and the capacity is decreasing. The future is dangerous, and it is truly unimaginable. If we want to seek urgent relief, the Hunan Provincial Government must follow President Chiang's proposal in the 20th year of the Republic to return the fields to the lake, and the recently promulgated Outline and Implementation Measures for the Consolidation of Farmland Water Conservancy by the Executive Yuan. Decisively prohibit construction and hope that the Economic Committee will comprehensively determine the water distribution area between Hunan and Hubei provinces, and no silt islands may continue to be reclaimed. The original island lake polders and dikes within the water distribution area should be abolished or restricted in height, so that they are one or two meters lower than the main dike, so as to avoid the increasing flood disaster, and the phenomenon that the Yangtze River rises slightly every year, and reports of floods are reported everywhere, officials and people are busy and panicked, and China and foreign countries are shocked can also be expected to be avoided.” (February 3)

Continued Criticism of Illegal Mining of Iron Ore Near Xiamen

Not Yet Proven That the Background is a Certain National; Provincial Government Sends Personnel to Survey and Start Mining

Xiamen Correspondence - It was reported earlier that Lu Zancheng, the head of the Jianyuanyuan Mining Cooperative, was mining without permission at the Saizai Mountain mine pit in Huli Village (also known as Zhukeng Lake Village) in the Heshan Special Zone outside Xiamen City. It has now been discovered that Lu signed a contract with Yang Fubin, the representative of the Yang surname villagers in Zhukeng Lake, on behalf of the cooperative, and Yang Qingmao, the village chief of Zhukeng Lake, signed as a witness. The contract was signed on December 23rd and 24th of last year. Mining exploration had already started half a month before the signing. By the time it was cracked down on January 19th, it had become a mine pit with a diameter of one zhang and a depth of seven zhang, with a horizontal excavation depth of two zhang at the bottom of the pit. According to Lu, the ore is manganese ore, but the Xiamen Star Daily reported at the time that it was tungsten ore and claimed that there was a background of a certain party, and the mined ore was being smuggled out of the port, etc. According to Liu Jitang, the director of the Special Zone Office, Lu had come to the office to register before excavating the mine, but had not yet been approved. Lu and others had already started work without authorization. This point is already illegal. The most important thing at present is whether Lu has a background or not, which must be strictly investigated. As for Yang Fubin and Yang Qingmao, they have been granted bail on the grounds of ignorance. Lu is still in custody. Lu's hometown is Quanzhou. As for whether his mining has a background, it has been more than half a month, and there is still no confirmation. It is still under investigation by the Special Zone Office. As for the quality of the ore in the pit, Chen Gaozhi, a technician sent by the Construction Department, confirmed that it was hard manganese, not tungsten ore. Lu and others had just approached the ore vein and had not yet reached the ore layer, so they had not yet had time to steal it. It is reported that hard manganese can be used for steelmaking. Although its need for military industrial is not as important as tungsten, it is also one of the military raw materials, so its value is very high. The provincial government has now sent technician Li Qishan to Xiamen in the coming days to conduct a detailed survey and start mining. As for the report here that a certain national is the background, it has not yet been proven. However, it is suspicious for a private individual to invest in mining exploration in order to seek uncertain profits. Also, the miner Li Wenying is currently a technician at the Anxi Zhongyu Mining Company and has lived in Taiwan. Whether he is Taiwanese and what kind of person he is, and the identity of an unknown shareholder in the cooperative, are all highly suspicious. (February 5).

Sichuan and Guangdong Provinces Purchase and Transport Large Quantities of Rice in Anhui

Anhui and Jiangxi Establish Tea Trade Company in Shanghai; Local Banks Provide Industrial and Commercial Loans

Wuhu Correspondence – Due to the bumper agricultural harvests in Anhui Province last year, the output of rice has increased sharply, the rural economy has been activated, and various businesses have also shown a trend of prosperity. Recently, during the abandoned lunar New Year, there is an unprecedented atmosphere of prosperity. The market is very stable, and the official support and promotion are even more exciting. I will describe the recent trends in rice and tea sales, and the status of local banks implementing industrial and commercial loans, so that you can know that Anhui Province's commerce and finance are making great efforts to move forward.

Guangdong Province has recently experienced another rice shortage, so officials and merchants are actively purchasing rice in Wuhu to transport to Guangdong to provide disaster relief for the people. Officials are commissioned by the Central Trust Bureau to be collected by the Wuhu Central Bank, and 45,000 shi have been purchased successively and transported. Recently, another 40,000 shi have been purchased and stored. Today, the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company will ship 20,000 shi by sea first. The merchants are the Guangchao rice shops stationed in Wuhu, who are also actively bidding for purchase. From autumn to now, over 1 million shi have been transported to Guangdong. According to statistics, various shops still have over 200,000 shi in stock waiting for transportation. However, at this time, Sichuan Province upstream has also experienced a serious rice shortage, and rice prices have soared, and there is no goods to meet the market. Therefore, the Sichuan Provincial Government has specially sent Commissioner Wei Wenhan and Chen Qidong, the section chief of the Agricultural Bureau, to Wuhu to purchase 30,000 shi of rice from Anhui to transport to Sichuan to rush for price control. The first batch of 5,500 shi has been exported yesterday, and purchases will continue in the future. The authorities of Anhui and Jiangxi provinces have decided to expand the sales of tea this year through consultation, and all measures have been determined. The Bank of Communications has decided to lend 2.5 million yuan, which will be paid by the Anhui Provincial Local Bank Jiangxi Yumin Bank. Recently, officials and businessmen in the two provinces have agreed to establish a tea trade company in Shanghai to facilitate sales abroad. The regulations are being drafted, and it can be established after the new tea is launched this year. As for manufacturing improvement, the government has decided to establish large-scale tea factories in the center of each tea-producing area, purchase machinery, and carry out rationalized large-scale manufacturing, so as to reduce costs and standardize quality, and compete with teas from India, Ceylon, and Java in the international market. The Qi Dou Tea Improvement Farm has compiled a design for a 10,000-box black tea manufacturing factory and submitted it to the Construction Department for review and implementation.

In order to promote the widespread development of industry and commerce, the Anhui Local Bank has specially launched small industrial and commercial loans. The total amount of loans is tentatively set at 20,000 yuan each in Wuhu, Huaining, and Bengbu, and 10,000 yuan each in Xuan city, Guangde, Nanling, Shouxian, Chu county, Hefei, and Shucheng. The maximum amount of each household loan is limited to 500 yuan, the term shall not exceed three months, and the monthly interest rate is 1%. Borrowers must seal up goods as collateral and must be guaranteed by the county government, chamber of commerce, or trade association. The Wuhu General Bank has telegraphed the above-mentioned branches or offices yesterday to carefully handle in accordance with the regulations and methods from now on. In addition, the bank plans to issue one-jiao, two-jiao, and five-jiao transfer notes, which are currently being printed and will be issued soon to regulate the market. (4th)

Robbery and Injury of Two People in Panqiao

On the night of the 3rd, twenty-odd robbers, speaking in Hakka dialect, dressed in short clothes, long robes, and worn-out military uniforms, robbed the house of Li Ke’ren, a farmer in Panqiao Township, District 3. They tied up Li, poured oil on him, and burned him, forcing him to reveal where he had hidden his money. His skin was burnt and festered. Li’s son sneaked out to beat a gong and raise the alarm. Upon hearing the sound, the villagers rushed to capture the robbers with farming tools. The robbers were ransacking boxes and cabinets. When the crowd arrived, they stopped robbing and fled. A villager named Wang Da bravely stepped forward to capture them, but was shot in the abdomen by the robbers. He immediately bled and fell to the ground. After the robbers left, he was sent to the Baolong Hospital in Shanghai for treatment. The bullet was still in his abdomen and had not been removed. His life was in danger. It is also heard that the loss from Li’s robbery was not small.

Tragedy of a Civil Ship Capsizing

Jin Hongqing, a 63-year-old farmer from Miaogang Township, District 3, had seven sons, all of whom had grown up, and the family was quite well-off. On the 4th, he took a boat to the southern town of Quanzhen to purchase a large batch of New Year's goods. On the way home at 4 pm, the boat passed through Wutangmen, and happened to meet a Huifeng steamship passing by. Hongqing immediately used a pole to hook the steamship's side, but the boat body was swaying and unstable. When it reached the turning point of the Duzhong Bridge, the whole boat capsized, and more than a dozen members of the family on the boat all fell into the river. Hongqing drowned on the spot, and the others were rescued. On the morning of the 5th, he and Tuzheng came to the city to report to the local court for examination.

Changzhou

Man Found Strangled in Wheat Field

A male body was found on the morning of the 4th in a wheat field near the Erxian Bridge, next to the Qishuyan to Henglin motor road in Lingang Township, District 5 of Wuyi. The man was about forty years old, wearing a vest and blue cloth pants, without shoes. There was a binding cloth around his neck, shaped like he had been murdered. No one claimed the body. The supervising officer Zhu Yuquan, together with the forensic doctor, went to the Police Sixth Precinct Office and telegraphed the local court to send personnel to the countryside for examination. The examination revealed that he had been strangled alive, and the village chief Xia Yinyue was ordered to claim the body, prepare a coffin, and collect the body. The cause of death may involve adultery and is currently under investigation.

Xiaoshan

Ancient Mirror Found on Hangwu Mountain

Zhao Jiujin, a resident of Hangwu Mountain, Xiaoshan Eastern Township, recently excavated an ancient tomb on the mountain and unearthed a platinum ancient mirror. Three antique dealers from Shaoxing purchased it for 500 yuan. The back is cast with human figures, dragons, and phoenixes, weighing four catties. The characters "Yongkang First Year" are faintly visible on the bricks in the cave. There are still many ancient objects that were purchased by antique dealers from outside.

Sports News

US University of California Joint Basketball Team Performs in Shanghai Last Night

Won Against Shanghai Mixed Team by Forty to Twenty-Eight Points; US Team's Swift and Well-Coordinated Moves Admirable

The University of California Joint Basketball Team, invited to perform in the Philippines, passed through Shanghai yesterday on their way back to the United States. The sports news department of the Western Shanghai Continental Daily specially invited them to give a performance and organized a Chinese-Western mixed team to compete against them last night at the Shen Garden. Throughout the game, the situation was extremely tense. In the second half, the score was tied four times, which shows its intensity. However, in the last three minutes, things took a sharp turn for the worse, and the American team scored twelve points in a row, thus defeating the Shanghai Mixed Team by a score of forty to twenty-eight. In the first half, the All-Star Team was only ahead by three points, with a score of eighteen to fifteen. Both sides showed their unique performances, which were exceptionally brilliant. The team will take the original Chichibu Maru to Japan today and then return to the United States.

The Color of the Visiting Team

The University of California team's tactics, like Shanghai's Mai Ling, are exceptionally swift. When they reach the opponent's basket, the five players move like a well-coordinated machine, seeking gaps to enter, and mostly shooting under the basket, rarely shooting from afar. They all wave their hands with a single hand and hit the basket. Unfortunately, there are still some deficiencies in their shooting accuracy, perhaps due to unfamiliarity with the venue or being in a foreign land for the first time. Center Howell, who is over six feet tall, is not particularly special. However, the two forwards, Browning and Moss, are terribly active. In a word, the team's technique is simply swift and well-coordinated.

The Shanghai Team is Very Good

The Shanghai Mixed Team invited Li Zhenzhong and Yin Hongxiang to Shanghai to help. It was not until a few minutes before the game that they arrived. The Shanghai Mixed Team is also made up entirely of all-stars. In the first half, they were unable to score many times due to a lack of coordination. Among the forwards, there was still something missing. Locke was too stiff, and Feng Nianhua was too short. However, the individual skills of the other four players, Li Zhenzhong, Shi Guiya, Yin Hongxiang, and Carson, were not inferior to those of the American team. The performances of Li, Yin, and Carson were particularly unique. The fierceness of their competition can be imagined to give the opponent four ties. If they add more well-coordinated teamwork, there is a great hope of defeating the American team.

Only Three Points Behind

Li Zhenzhong's jump ball was not weaker than the opponent's tall man. After the game started, Yin Hongxiang got the first throwing opportunity, but unfortunately it did not go in. Moss fouled, and Yin first made a free throw, opening the record. As it was for several minutes, they failed to score. After the American team called a timeout, Li Zhenzhong added two more points, and the Shanghai team suddenly took the lead with a score of three to zero. The game was tense, and the American team did not seem to score. The difference between the two sides was only one, two, or three points. The Shanghai team was only slightly behind. The American team added Widdis to replace center Howell, and the Shanghai team also replaced Locke with Shi Guiya. At the end of the first half, the American team was only ahead by three points with a score of eighteen to fifteen.

Tied Four Times

At the beginning of the second half, Locke replaced Feng Nianhua, and Howell was re-appointed as the opponent's center. Both sides committed numerous fouls, each scoring with free throws. Carson and Li Zhenzhong scored three free throws in a row, and the Shanghai team made their first tie at eighteen each. The performances of both sides entered a better state, with scores of eighteen each, twenty each, and even twenty-six each, and the shape of the match was extremely tense. At this time, Yin Hongxiang got a chance to foul the opposing captain Browning, but unexpectedly, he missed both free throws, which was a pity. On the other hand, Browning waved his hand with a single hand and scored, and the American team was two points ahead again with a score of twenty-eight to twenty-six. Carson scored, and it was a tie again. With only three minutes left to the end, the American team suddenly showed their power, and Browning and Howell scored one after another, so their momentum became unstoppable. The Shanghai team lost twelve points in a row and lost by a score of twenty-eight to forty.

The Battle of Manila

(A dispatch from our reporter in the Philippines, Yan Wenchou)

(Special Dispatch from Manila) The Philippine Amateur Athletic Federation, in order to enhance the observation of the Philippine basketball team, specifically invited the alumni basketball team of the University of Southern California to come to Manila for eight matches. The team accepted the invitation and arrived in Manila on the eleventh day of the first month, a group of eight people. Except for one player who was a basketball player from the University of Iowa, the rest were all players from the University of California. However, none of them had attended the World Games this time. Their physique was extraordinary and mighty, the tallest being six feet one inch, and the shortest being five feet nine inches. The heaviest weighed one hundred and ninety pounds, and the lightest weighed one hundred and sixty-five pounds, which were indeed unmatched by Orientals. The guard could almost reach the basket with a single jump. The result of the matches was seven wins and one loss. Their loss was only by one point, which can also be said to be a complete victory. The results of each match are detailed below:

President's Reception

On the day of arrival in Manila, they went straight to the Presidential Palace to pay respects to Philippine President Quezon. Due to his ill health, the Secretary-General came out to receive them. President Quezon granted another audience on the morning of the twelfth, extending great comfort to the team for their long journey. They stayed at the YMCA of the U.S. Army and Navy in the Philippines. The Athletic Federation wholeheartedly took on the responsibility of entertaining them.

Changing Basketball Skills

During the first match, they played lightly and sketched casually, without any effort, which greatly dissatisfied the audience. It seemed that with such slow passing, they would definitely be defeated by the Philippine team. Sure enough, in the second match against the Philippine basketball runner-up, the San Beda University team, they lost by a narrow margin. The general audience was even more disappointed. In the third match, the Philippine basketball champion team, the San Sebastian College–Recoletos team, which has always been known for its iron army, came out to play. The Philippine team that attended this World Games was based on this team. That night, the audience was especially large. Before the tip-off at 1:30, all the seats were filled, and more than a thousand people could not get in. The psychology of the audience this time was to watch the San Sebastian College–Recoletos players show off their skills and defeat this burly and mighty American team, not leaving a single piece of armor intact. However, the reality was even more unexpected. That night, the American team, also at a critical juncture where its reputation was at stake, changed its strategy, focusing on tight passing and accurate shooting to win. Despite the San Sebastian College–Recoletos team's exhausted screams and the cheers of the Filipino crowd throughout the arena, they were ultimately unable to reverse the defeat.

Crowded Audience

After defeating the champion San Sebastian College–Recoletos team, the fans were even more excited. Therefore, the seats for the fourth, fifth, sixth, and seventh matches were all reserved in advance. The Rizal Memorial Basketball Coliseum can only accommodate more than 8,000 spectators, divided into four classes with prices of one peso and five centavos, one peso and two centavos, eight centavos, and four centavos. The first two classes of seats have numbers and can be reserved in advance. The third and fourth classes are seated on a first-come, first-served basis. Because there was a problem of overcrowding in the third and fourth matches, those who arrived late were left out. Therefore, later, people brought bread to fill their stomachs and occupy seats three hours before the start of the game. The arena also widely set up bulletin boards, and the results of each point were announced outside, so that those who could not get in could also know the situation in the arena and feel comforted rather than running in vain.

Audience's Mischief

Filipinos watch basketball games entirely to cheer for their own side, without respecting the visiting team. In the past, when our country's teams went to the Philippines to compete, the bad impressions were always caused by the Filipino audience's unreasonable jeering, which aroused the dissatisfaction of the overseas Chinese audience and led to disputes. This time, they also wanted to use unreasonable ridicule to make the American team angry and disrupt their formation. In the seventh match against the World Games team, when the Filipino referee penalized the Philippine team with a free throw, the audience was in an uproar, accusing him of being unfair and throwing fruit peels and miscellaneous objects into the arena like butterflies flying around. The police also didn't know whether to laugh or cry and couldn't stop them, forcing the American team to almost leave the arena immediately and end the game. Fortunately, the authorities of the Athletic Federation came out to explain everything before the game could continue to the end. In the eighth match, until the end of the second quarter, the Philippine team was leading by four points, and the audience cheered wildly, almost shaking the walls, thinking that they could avenge their shame. Unexpectedly, the American team responded calmly and showed amazing skills, finally turning defeat into victory, which made thousands of Filipinos very dejected.

Filipino Revenue

The round-trip expenses for the American team this time were only about 8,000 Philippine pesos. It is estimated that nearly 30,000 pesos can be collected from the eight matches. The surplus earned by the Athletic Federation this time is considerable.

Zhu Qiliang Wins Amateur Billiards Group A Championship

Result: 2,000 Points vs. 1,961 Points Zhang Yingda Strived Repeatedly but Ultimately Failed

Zhu Qiliang, with his calm spirit and careful technique, finally defeated Zhang Yingda in the extremely tense final stage, reaching the 2,000-point mark first and winning this year's Shanghai Amateur Billiards Group A Championship. This is also the great reward for Zhu's years of hard work and practice, and his golden age is gradually appearing. Zhu should strive for further progress to achieve greater success.

Zhu's initial victory over Ding Mingyi relied on good luck. At that time, Zhu was more than 150 points behind, but in the last few shots, Zhu took the lead. In the semi-finals, Zhu calmly defeated Wu Chengxiang and won the right to the finals. In the final four matches, Zhu benefited from the second match, winning more than 220 points. In the first and third matches, the two sides were neck and neck, with limited differences. The fourth match was quite unfavorable, but fortunately, he had won too many points. Even when he was at a disadvantage, he was still able to cheer up and maintain his composure. The championship title belonged to him. At the beginning of this Group A Championship, Medina was originally the most popular, followed by Zhang Yingda and Ding Mingyi. Unexpectedly, Zhu Qiliang emerged as a dark horse, defeating Ding and Zhang in succession and replacing them. This can be said to be an anomaly.

Zhang Yingda, last year's runner-up, was once again controlled by his bad luck and missed the golden opportunity. In the last 100-point competition, he still ranked second. When the third match started yesterday, the two sides were on the same level. The fourth match then changed greatly. Zhang went from being 235 points behind (1290 vs. 1545) to discovering huge scores of 65, 34, 45, 34, 37, etc., winning more than 40 points and surpassing Zhu (1716 vs. 1676). Unexpectedly, Zhang was careless many times and missed many good opportunities. Zhu then soared again, scoring 79 points in one shot and taking the lead again. From then on, Zhang was still in adversity, following behind Zhu. When the score reached 1909 vs. 1971, another opportunity for a comeback came. He had already scored 52 points in one shot. Unexpectedly, at the critical moment, he missed the opportunity. Zhu then reached the final goal of 2,000 points, winning only 39 points more than Zhang Yingda. The last match lasted the longest, starting at 9:15 and ending at 12:45.

City Museum to Hold Exhibition of Museums from Various Countries

Starting from February 11th

Since the opening of the Shanghai City Museum on the 10th of last month, people from all over the world have praised the museum's excellent display, beautiful collection, and well-organized management. The number of visitors every day is very crowded. The heads of museums, people's education centers, exhibition halls, and school laboratories from all over the country have personally come to the museum to learn everything or send letters to the museum to conduct special discussions. Now that the new semester has begun in various schools, dozens of schools of all levels are scheduling visits every day. The museum is open all year round except for Tuesdays. During the Lunar New Year, there will be many visitors. It is recently learned that the first special exhibition of the museum has been decided to be held from the 11th of this month (i.e., the day of the Lunar New Year). After consultation with the Chinese Museum Association, the film of museums from various countries collected by the Association and the Hallum Lee has been sent to Shanghai, and a special exhibition of the museum's collected materials will be held. There are more than 1,000 exhibits in total. Photos and books of the exterior and interior of famous museums in various countries around the world, as well as representative exhibits, are displayed, so that viewers can understand the concept of the development of museum undertakings in various countries in the modern era and recognize the richness of museum collections in various countries. In a few hours, it is like traveling around the world. In addition, the museum's display uses the most advanced methods of our country's museums, so those who pay attention to the display of shop windows and the decoration of family rooms should also go and take a look to learn from it. It is the best place to relax and enjoy during the Lunar New Year.

Ministry of Education Formulates Measures to Promote Vocational Supplementary Education

(Nanjing, 5th) The Ministry of Education issued an order to all departments and bureaus, stating that the promotion of vocational education in various provinces and cities has recently laid a foundation. However, it is urgent to supplement the knowledge and skills that workers and apprentices who are already engaged in vocational work should have in order to increase work efficiency. Those who volunteer to engage in vocational work will be taught vocational knowledge and skills so that they can have the opportunity to serve. The Ministry has promulgated the regulations on vocational supplementary schools and ordered them to be followed. In the past three years, various provinces and cities have paid little attention to this educational facility. Now, the Ministry has formulated the outline of measures for various provinces and cities to promote vocational supplementary education and issued them together. Please follow them and prepare detailed implementation measures before the end of March and submit them to the Ministry for approval. The main points of the outline of measures for vocational supplementary education are as follows:

1. The educational administrative organs of all provinces and cities should follow the provisions of this outline of measures to earnestly promote vocational supplementary education and prepare detailed implementation measures and submit them to the Ministry for record.

2. Regarding the establishment of vocational supplementary schools, 甲. All vocational schools, rural normal schools, and secondary normal schools with special labor equipment should make use of their original equipment and talents to do their best to run vocational supplementary schools with the same nature as the schools. 乙. Universities and specialized schools should hold advanced vocational primary supplementary classes or short-term vocational training classes to provide in-depth subject supplementary studies for those who already have jobs. 丙. All vocational groups in various industries should cooperate with vocational schools and other equivalent schools to make use of school equipment to run vocational supplementary schools or vocational training classes related to this industry. Those industries that have not organized groups should quickly organize and hold this major industry. 凡. Universities, specialized schools, vocational schools, and rural normal schools that run vocational supplementary education should be listed as extension undertakings. The number of classes run should be determined according to the capacity of the school's equipment. The location of the school is not limited to the school. 戊. The subjects attached to vocational supplementary schools at all levels should, in addition to being of the same nature as the schools, also pay close attention to the needs of the local area. The attached subjects, such as agricultural vocational schools and rural normal schools, should run agronomy, animal husbandry, cooperation, and other subjects. Vocational and girls' secondary normal schools should run home economics, childcare, sewing, and domestic helper subjects. 己. The surplus of vocational supplementary schools and vocational training classes should all comply with the provisions of the regulations on vocational supplementary schools and the interim measures for short-term vocational training classes promulgated by the Ministry.

3. Regarding the teachers of vocational supplementary schools, 甲. In addition to the teachers designated by the school to teach, the vocational supplementary schools or vocational training classes attached to schools at all levels can also select high-grade students with excellent grades to assist in teaching. When necessary, technical personnel and artists from various industries may be hired to teach. 乙. The teaching subjects of vocational supplementary schools and vocational training classes should be in accordance with the regulations of vocational supplementary schools and the interim measures for short-term vocational training classes promulgated by the Ministry.

4. Regarding the funding of vocational supplementary schools, 甲. The funding for vocational supplementary schools or vocational training classes run by schools at all levels should be based on the principle of saving expenses from the original budget. The expenses for practical materials and hiring full-time teachers may be requested from the competent authorities for subsidies when necessary. The funding for vocational supplementary schools or vocational training classes run by vocational groups should be raised by the groups themselves. If the operation is successful, they may apply to the competent authorities for appropriate subsidies. 5. Regarding the implementation steps of vocational supplementary schools, 甲. All provinces and cities should first select appropriate schools in the prosperous industrial and commercial areas of the provinces and cities to run vocational supplementary schools or vocational training classes. After they are successful, they should gradually expand and establish them. 乙. In the 26th year of the Republic of China, all vocational schools, rural normal schools, and vocational groups in various specialized schools and above, except for those that have been approved to postpone by the competent educational administrative organs due to special circumstances, should be held. 丙. All provinces and cities should register and assess technicians in various industries and, when necessary, concentrate them for short-term training to determine the preparation of teachers for vocational supplementary schools.

Sino-Soviet Cultural Association

Held a Board Meeting Yesterday

(Nanjing, 5th) The Sino-Soviet Cultural Association held its ninth board meeting yesterday and decided to hold a centennial commemoration of the death of the great Russian poet Alexander Pushkin on the 9th. The program includes a report on Pushkin's life, a reading of the original poems in Russian, and a screening of films. In addition, Yang Hu and 18 others were approved as members. The Sino-Soviet Cultural Association commemorated the Pushkin Centennial on the 10th of this month. President Sun Ke sent a telegram to the Moscow News and Pravda, saying that Pushkin's immortal achievements, such as the genius of a poet (using the virtuous and inspiring good senses), writings, and the freedom of oppressed nations, are extremely valuable. I am in charge of the Sino-Soviet Cultural Association and other Chinese social groups, and I am using this grand ceremony to hold commemorative meetings, publish special issues of magazines and collections of essays, and print new Chinese translations of Pushkin's masterpieces to universally introduce Pushkin's life and writings to our country. I firmly believe that this kind of cultural communication and mutual understanding has great significance in general politics.

Social Bureau Investigates 453 Private Schools in the City

Reorganize after Registration is Completed

In order to rectify and improve private schools, the Municipal Social Bureau held a general survey of private schools throughout the city in December last year. Now it is over. There are a total of 453 private schools in the city, with Zhabei having the most, with 197 schools, 56 schools in Nanshi, 46 schools in Yangjing, 50 schools in Fahua, 70 schools in Yinxiang, 18 schools in Tangqiao, 7 schools in Zhenru, 4 schools in Yangsi, 3 schools in Gaohang, and 1 school each in Gaoqiao and Jiangwan. There are a total of 453 teachers, of which 6 are women. The teachers are mostly from the Jiangbei area, such as Yancheng, Gaoyou, Liuhe, and Dongtai, accounting for about nine-tenths of the total. The total number of students receiving private school education in the city is about 11,000. Each private school accommodates a maximum of 60 or 70 people and a minimum of about 5 or 6 people. The average tuition fee for students is about 4 yuan for the large ones, 1 yuan for the medium ones, and 1 yuan for the small ones. The general registration of private schools is now being carried out. In recent days, the teachers have been very enthusiastic about going to the Municipal Social Bureau in the city center to register. The Bureau will wait until the registration is completed before proceeding with the third step of the reorganization work.

Local News

Wang Jingwei Arrived in Shanghai by Plane Yesterday from Nanjing

Chen Bijun, Zeng Zhongming, and Others Came Along. Song Ziwen and Gu Mengyu Visited.

According to the Central News Agency, Wang Jingwei, Chairman of the Central Political Council, arrived in Shanghai by Ford aircraft at 11:35 AM yesterday morning, accompanied by his wife, Ms. Chen Bijun, Central Committee member Zeng Zhongming, attending physician Luo Guanglin, and seven secretaries and nurses, due to private matters awaiting his attention in Shanghai. After disembarking, he went to the residence of Central Committee member Chu Minyi to rest. Song Ziwen, Standing Committee member of the National Economic Council, and Gu Mengyu, Secretary-General of the Central Political Council, and others visited him successively. The details of Wang's arrival in Shanghai are recorded as follows:

Welcoming Personnel

After the exhibition, it can be sold, which is an excellent way to increase exports. Your bureau has always vigorously promoted the export of national products. If you can find a way to invite major domestic merchants to participate, please telegraph in advance so that the association can be notified, and a showroom will be reserved for our country. Based on this, it is found that this tableware exhibition held in Prague, Czech Republic, can be used to promote my country's excellent products so that foreigners can recognize them, and it will also be beneficial to promote trade in the future. The letter is approved, and in addition to sending separate letters, a corresponding letter is sent to your association for reference. Please forward it to relevant manufacturers, carefully select exhibits for application, and please reply quickly for summary."

The Sino-Siamese Association is About to be Established

The Siamese Side Has Been Established

According to the Central News Agency, since the exchange of inspection groups between China and Siam, the diplomatic relations have been cordial and the relationship has become closer. The governments and people of the two countries initiated the establishment of the Sino-Siamese Association to communicate culture and connect feelings. In our country, Weng Wenhao, Zhang Qun, and members of the inspection group Ling Bing are preparing, and it will be established soon. In Siam, it has been established through the efforts of people from the country and overseas Chinese in Siam. The articles of association and commemorative photos of its establishment have been received here. It is said that the responsible persons are important members of the country's government and the president of our chamber of commerce. The articles of association of the association are recorded as follows: Article 1: This association is named the Sino-Siamese Association. Article 2: The temporary general meeting address of this association is located in the Chinese General Chamber of Commerce on Sathorn Road, Bangkok. Article 3: The purpose is to promote Sino-Siamese culture and connect the feelings of the Sino-Siamese people. Article 4: The members of this association are divided into two types: A. Ordinary members; B. Honorary members. Article 5: Ordinary members: (1) Founders of this association; (2) Those who join as members in accordance with the articles of association of this association. The above members shall pay a monthly membership fee of half a baht. Those who pay one hundred baht at a time shall be permanent members. Article 6: Honorary members are those invited by this association. Those who are invited by this association to be honorary chairmen are naturally honorary members. Article 7: Ordinary members have the right to attend, propose, and vote at each general meeting, and may provide and instruct the executive committee on all association affairs. Article 8: Ordinary members and honorary members have the right to use the association's address in accordance with the regulations stipulated in the association's rules. Article 9: Reasons for members to withdraw from membership: (1) Voluntary resignation; (2) Death; (3) With a two-thirds vote of the executive committee, the member's behavior is sufficient to cause significant losses to this association. Article 10: The executive officers of the association are as follows: A. General Assembly of Members; B. Executive Committee. Article 11: The General Assembly of Members has the power to approve the annual settlement and entrustment and supervise the executive committee. Article 12: The annual general meeting of members shall be held once a year. An extraordinary general meeting may be convened when the executive committee deems it appropriate or when no less than fifteen members request it. The quorum for the General Assembly of Members shall be one-fifth of the total number of members or no less than thirty people. Article 13: When the annual general meeting of members is held, the executive committee shall submit the annual settlement and report on the progress of association affairs. Article 14: When the annual general meeting of members is held, the general meeting shall elect a chairman of the executive committee, and then the chairman shall elect twenty members from all members to submit to the general meeting for approval as executive committee members. The executive committee members shall elect a vice-chairman, secretary, treasurer, and other necessary officers. Article 15: The executive committee shall hold a meeting at least once a month, and a quorum of at least seven people shall be present. Article 16: The term of office of the executive committee member is one year, but they may be re-elected. When there is a vacancy on the executive committee, the chairman of the executive committee shall elect a member to fill the vacancy. The term of office of the supplementary executive committee member shall terminate when the term of office of the original executive

Committee member expires. Article 17: The executive committee member performs his duties under the trust of the general assembly of members and has the right to stipulate various detailed rules. Article 18: An executive committee member shall naturally leave office under the following circumstances: 1. Term expires; 2. Resignation; 3. Death; 4. Withdrawal from membership; 5. The general assembly of members votes to remove him from office. Article 19: This article of association shall be added, deleted, or amended by a vote of three-quarters of the members present at the general assembly of members.

A Glimpse of the Achievements of the National Economic Council's Cotton Control Commission Since its Establishment

Promote Cotton Production and Improve Quality, Strive to Export and Save Imports

The National Economic Council's Cotton Control Commission has been established for three years. Its mission is to promote cotton production and improve quality, not only to achieve self-sufficiency but also to strive for exports to save imports and develop the national economy. Last year, my country's cotton harvest increased significantly, which is the result of the commission's three years of hard work. Other efforts, such as textile experiments, are also in progress. The details are described as follows:

Main Work

The main work of the Cotton Control Commission is to promote cotton fields and improve quality. Therefore, the Central Cotton Production Improvement Institute was first established, and a cotton farm was set up in Xiaolingwei, Nanjing, to engage in fine-staple upland cotton and German-American cotton breeding and various research work. A breeding and propagation farm was attached to Dongtai to plant Golden American cotton. Subsequently, cotton production improvement institutes were established in Henan, Shaanxi, Hubei, Hebei, Shanxi, and other provinces, with thirteen cotton farms attached to cultivate Sizi, Tuozi, Dezi, and Jinzi American cotton and Lingbao cotton for breeding and propagation to meet the needs of promotion. In the past few years, the number of acres of American cotton promoted in Jiangsu, Henan, Shaanxi, Shanxi, Hubei, Hebei, Gansu, and other provinces totaled 570,200 mu in the 23rd year, 1,288,454 mu in the 24th year, and 2,676,025 mu in the 25th year. Among them, Shaanxi Province accounted for the largest number of acres. After the strict implementation of the prohibition of opium cultivation, changing to cotton cultivation was the most suitable crop, so the increase in cotton fields was particularly rapid. Jiangsu Province promoted American cotton the earliest, reaching 300,000 mu in the 23rd year and 600,000 mu in the 25th year, an increase of one time. Henan and Shanxi provinces increased by about ten times. Other provinces have gradually promoted it after the establishment of the provincial improvement institutes, and the number is also very large.

Organize Cooperatives

In order to facilitate promotion, the association guided farmers in various provinces to organize cooperatives. In Jiangsu, Shaanxi, Henan, Shanxi, and Hebei provinces, there were a total of 40 cooperatives in the 23rd year, with a total of 23,444 members and a total of 308,685 mu of cotton fields. In the 24th year, it increased to 75 cooperatives, with a total of 53,059 members and 856,668 mu of cotton fields. Last year, there were not many changes in Jiangsu, Shaanxi, Henan, and Shanxi provinces. Hebei Province added nearly 700 cooperatives, and Hubei Province newly organized about 190 cooperatives. The two provinces added about 50,000 members and about 500,000 mu of cotton fields. The cooperative loans are provided by the China Agricultural Cooperative Loan Syndicate organized by the banking community in this city. The total amount of loans in the past three years is about 4 million yuan. To facilitate the sale of cotton by various cooperatives, the association has established a cotton transportation and sales office in Shanghai. In the past three years, it has handled the sale of about 100,000 dan of cotton.

Improve Cotton Spinning

In order to study and improve the cotton spinning industry, there has long been a proposal to establish a cotton industry experiment hall. At that time, the National Central Research Institute also had a plan to set up a textile experiment factory. After consultation, it was decided to jointly establish it. A certain area was designated in the south of the Institute of Science and Technology of the Central Research Institute in Shanghai, and construction began at the end of the 23rd year. The total budget was 1.2 million yuan in national currency, divided into three phases. The initial equipment cost was 400,000 yuan, the base construction cost was 160,000 yuan, and the construction and equipment cost was 240,000 yuan. By July of the 25th year, the factory buildings were built, and the textile machines were selected and purchased from various countries, including 31 units for the spinning department, such as various cleaning, combing, fine combing, roving, and spinning machines, and 71 units for the weaving department, such as various winding, jacquard, and fabric finishing machines. They were also installed and tested one after another at this time. At first, 42-count double-strand yarn was spun and ordinary fine cloth was woven. Now, 50-60 count yarn is being spun and various fine products such as straight tribute flannel and jacquard are being woven. The experiment department is equipped with various cotton fiber testing machines, yarn count measuring scales, temperature measuring scales, cotton yarn and cotton cloth strength and elongation testing machines, and more than 70 fabric bursting, ventilation, waterproof shrinkage, and length dyeing fastness instruments, mainly to test the products of each department of the hall. Many people outside also said that they wanted to request analysis and inspection.

The Elevation of the Status of the Chinese and Belgian Envoys Will Be Realized This Autumn

Jules D'Anethan Will No Longer Return to His Post

According to sources in diplomatic circles here, the relationship between China and Belgium has become increasingly close in recent years. The authorities of the two countries are currently proceeding with the elevation of the status of their envoys to each other. Before his vacation back to his country last year, Jules D'Anethan, the Belgian Minister to China, had several consultations with the authorities of our Ministry of Foreign Affairs, and both parties expressed their approval. However, after the status of the envoys is elevated, all light expenses will inevitably increase accordingly, so it must be approved by the central meetings of both countries before it can be realized. Minister D'Anethan has reported the results of his several consultations with our Ministry to the Belgian authorities after returning to his country. It is expected that it can be realized this autumn. After Minister D'Anethan returned to his country, he has been transferred to an internal position and it has been decided that he will no longer come to China.
